    function initAutocomplete() {
      window.autocomplete = new google.maps.places.Autocomplete(document.getElementById('autocomplete'), {types: ['geocode']});
      window.autocomplete.addListener('place_changed', explicitSearch);
    }

    var explicitSearch = function() {
      var place = window.autocomplete.getPlace();

      window.user_location["address"]= place["formatted_address"];
      window.user_location["address_latitude"]= place.geometry.location.lat();
      window.user_location["address_longitude"]= place.geometry.location.lng();

      CorpSiteSearch.updateResultsList(true);
      document.dispatchEvent(new Event('search_complete'));
    }
